  "new_str": "## Experiment Implementation Plan\n\n### Overview\nThis experiment evaluates **inference-time temperature annealing** for LLM calibration - the key unimplemented novelty from the refined hypothesis. We compare 5 methods on 3 datasets (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\n\n1. **Uncalibrated baseline**: Standard softmax on logits\n2. **Temperature Scaling (TS)**: Post-hoc calibration with single temperature parameter\n3. **Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)**: Post-hoc calibration using entropy adjustments  \n4. **Annealing + Softmax**: Inference-time per-class temperature annealing\n5. **Annealing + TEC**: Combine annealing with post-hoc TEC\n\n### Key Technical Challenge\nThe method requires access to **logits** (pre-softmax activations) to apply per-class temperature scaling. API-based LLMs (OpenRouter) typically don't expose logits, so we use **local HuggingFace models**.\n\n### Phase 0: Setup (30 minutes)\n\n1. **Install dependencies**:\n```bash\npip install torch transformers datasets numpy pandas scikit-learn matplotlib seaborn tqdm\n```\n\n2. **Load datasets** from dependency:\n- Path: `/ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_3fUR0i5e8NC7/3_invention_loop/iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json`\n- Use 3 datasets: SST-2 (2 classes), AG News (4 classes), DBpedia (14 classes)\n- Create train/val/test splits: 70%/15%/15% with stratified sampling\n\n3. **Load pretrained models** (local, for logit access):\n- SST-2: `textattack/bert-base-uncased-SST-2` \n- AG News: `textattack/roberta-base-ag-news`\n- DBpedia: Train a simple classifier on sentence embeddings (see fallback plan)\n\n### Phase 1: Implement Calibration Methods (1.5 hours)\n\n**Core function - Temperature Annealing**:\n```python\nimport torch\nimport torch.nn as nn\nimport torch.nn.functional as F\n\ndef anneal_temperature(num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute per-class temperature: T(c) = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule(c/C)\n    \n    Args:\n        num_classes: Number of classes C\n        T_start: Starting temperature (higher = more uniform distribution)\n        T_end: Ending temperature (lower = sharper distribution)\n        schedule_type: 'linear', 'exponential', or 'physics'\n    \n    Returns:\n        T_c: Tensor of shape (num_classes,) with per-class temperatures\n    \"\"\"\n    c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\n    x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\n    \n    if schedule_type == 'linear':\n        schedule = 1.0 - x  # Linear decay\n    elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\n        schedule = torch.exp(-x)  # Exponential decay\n    elif schedule_type == 'physics':\n        # Physics-inspired: 1/log(1 + x*(e-1))\n        schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown schedule: {schedule_type}\")\n    \n    T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\n    return T_c\n\n# Test the function\nT_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes=4, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear')\nprint(f\"Linear schedule T_c: {T_c}\")  # Should be [2.0, 1.75, 1.5, 1.25] approx\n```\n\n**Method 1: Uncalibrated Baseline**:\n```python\ndef uncalibrated_predict(logits):\n    \"\"\"Standard softmax without calibration.\"\"\"\n    return F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\n```\n\n**Method 2: Temperature Scaling (TS)**:\n```python\nclass TemperatureScaling:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\n    \n    def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n        \"\"\"Optimize temperature on validation set using NLL loss.\"\"\"\n        optimizer = torch.optim.LBFGS([self.temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\n        \n        for _ in range(100):\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            scaled_logits = val_logits / self.temperature\n            loss = F.cross_entropy(scaled_logits, val_labels)\n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step(lambda: F.cross_entropy(val_logits / self.temperature, val_labels))\n        \n        return self.temperature.item()\n    \n    def calibrate(self, logits):\n        \"\"\"Apply optimized temperature to logits.\"\"\"\n        return F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\n```\n\n**Method 3: Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)**:\n```python\nclass ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\n        self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\n    \n    def compute_entropy(self, probs):\n        \"\"\"Shannon entropy: H = -sum(p * log(p))\"\"\"\n        return -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\n    \n    def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n        \"\"\"Optimize temperature and entropy weight on validation set.\"\"\"\n        optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\n        \n        for epoch in range(100):\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            \n            # Scale logits by temperature\n            scaled_logits = val_logits / self.temperature\n            probs = F.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\n            \n            # Compute entropy and adjust probabilities\n            entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\n            adjusted_probs = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\n            adjusted_probs = adjusted_probs / adjusted_probs.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n            \n            # NLL loss on adjusted probabilities\n            loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted_probs + 1e-10), val_labels)\n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step()\n        \n        return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\n    \n    def calibrate(self, logits):\n        \"\"\"Apply TEC to logits.\"\"\"\n        probs = F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\n        entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\n        adjusted = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight.item() * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\n        adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n        return adjusted\n```\n\n**Method 4: Annealing + Softmax (Core Novelty)**:\n```python\nclass AnnealingSoftmax:\n    def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\n        self.T_start = T_start\n        self.T_end = T_end\n        self.schedule_type = schedule_type\n    \n    def calibrate(self, logits):\n        \"\"\"\n        Apply per-class temperature annealing during inference.\n        \n        Args:\n            logits: Tensor of shape (batch_size, num_classes)\n        \n        Returns:\n            probs: Calibrated probabilities of shape (batch_size, num_classes)\n        \"\"\"\n        num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\n        \n        # Compute per-class temperatures\n        T_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes, self.T_start, self.T_end, self.schedule_type)\n        # T_c shape: (num_classes,)\n        \n        # Expand to batch size\n        T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)\n        # T_c_batch shape: (batch_size, num_classes)\n        \n        # Scale logits by per-class temperature\n        annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\n        \n        # Apply softmax\n        probs = F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\n        return probs\n```\n\n**Method 5: Annealing + Post-hoc TEC**:\n```python\nclass AnnealingPlusTEC:\n    def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\n        self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\n        self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\n    \n    def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n        \"\"\"First anneal, then apply TEC on annealed outputs.\"\"\"\n        # Apply annealing\n        annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\n        val_annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\n        \n        # Convert back to logits for TEC\n        annealed_logits = torch.log(annealed_probs + 1e-10)\n        val_annealed_logits = torch.log(val_annealed_probs + 1e-10)\n        \n        # Fit TEC\n        T_opt, w_opt = self.tec.fit(annealed_logits, labels, val_annealed_logits, val_labels)\n        return T_opt, w_opt\n    \n    def calibrate(self, logits):\n        \"\"\"Apply annealing then TEC.\"\"\"\n        annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\n        # Apply TEC adjustment to annealed probabilities\n        entropy = self.tec.compute_entropy(annealed_probs)\n        adjusted = annealed_probs * (1 + self.tec.entropy_weight.item() * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\n        adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n        return adjusted\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Hyperparameter Search (1.5 hours)\n\n**Grid search over annealing parameters**:\n```python\nparam_grid = {\n    'T_start': [1.0, 2.0, 5.0],\n    'T_end': [0.5, 1.0],\n    'schedule_type': ['linear', 'exponential', 'physics']\n}\n\nbest_params = {}\nbest_ece = float('inf')\n\nfor T_start in param_grid['T_start']:\n    for T_end in param_grid['T_end']:\n        for schedule in param_grid['schedule_type']:\n            # Create method with these parameters\n            method = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule)\n            \n            # Calibrate validation set\n            val_probs = method.calibrate(val_logits)\n            val_preds = torch.argmax(val_probs, dim=-1)\n            val_confs = torch.max(val_probs, dim=-1).values\n            \n            # Compute ECE\n            val_ece = compute_ece(val_confs, val_preds, val_labels)\n            \n            # Check if best\n            if val_ece < best_ece:\n                best_ece = val_ece\n                best_params = {'T_start': T_start, 'T_end': T_end, 'schedule': schedule}\n\nprint(f\"Best parameters: {best_params}, ECE: {best_ece:.4f}\")\n```\n\n**Use validation set for tuning** - do NOT use test set for hyperparameter selection.\n\n### Phase 3: Evaluation Metrics (45 minutes)\n\n**Implement ECE (Expected Calibration Error)**:\n```python\ndef compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute Expected Calibration Error.\n    \n    Args:\n        confidences: Tensor of shape (n_samples,) with max probability per sample\n        predictions: Tensor of shape (n_samples,) with predicted class per sample\n        labels: Tensor of shape (n_samples,) with true class per sample\n        num_bins: Number of bins for calibration curve\n    \n    Returns:\n        ece: Scalar ECE value\n    \"\"\"\n    bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\n    ece = 0.0\n    \n    for i in range(num_bins):\n        # Get samples in this bin\n        mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\n        \n        if mask.sum() > 0:\n            # Accuracy and confidence for this bin\n            bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\n            bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\n            \n            # Weighted calibration gap\n            ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\n    \n    return ece.item()\n```\n\n**Implement Brier Score**:\n```python\ndef compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute Brier Score (mean squared error of probability predictions).\n    \n    Args:\n        probs: Tensor of shape (n_samples, n_classes)\n        labels: Tensor of shape (n_samples,)\n    \n    Returns:\n        brier: Scalar Brier score\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = probs.shape[0]\n    n_classes = probs.shape[1]\n    \n    # One-hot encode labels\n    one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=n_classes).float()\n    \n    # Compute Brier score\n    brier = torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2)\n    return brier.item()\n```\n\n**Implement NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood)**:\n```python\ndef compute_nll(probs, labels):\n    \"\"\"Compute Negative Log-Likelihood.\"\"\"\n    return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\n```\n\n### Phase 4: Run Experiments (1.5 hours)\n\n**Main experiment loop**:\n```python\nresults = {}\n\nfor dataset_name in ['sst-2', 'ag_news', 'dbpedia']:\n    print(f\"\\n{'='*60}\")\n    print(f\"Dataset: {dataset_name}\")\n    print(f\"{'='*60}\")\n    \n    # Load data\n    train_data, val_data, test_data = load_and_split_data(dataset_name)\n    \n    # Get logits from pretrained model\n    model = load_pretrained_model(dataset_name)\n    train_logits = get_logits(model, train_data)\n    val_logits = get_logits(model, val_data)\n    test_logits = get_logits(model, test_data)\n    \n    # Get labels\n    train_labels = torch.tensor([ex['label'] for ex in train_data])\n    val_labels = torch.tensor([ex['label'] for ex in val_data])\n    test_labels = torch.tensor([ex['label'] for ex in test_data])\n    \n    # Evaluate each method\n    dataset_results = {}\n    \n    # Method 1: Uncalibrated\n    uncal_probs = uncalibrated_predict(test_logits)\n    dataset_results['uncalibrated'] = compute_metrics(uncal_probs, test_labels)\n    \n    # Method 2: Temperature Scaling\n    ts = TemperatureScaling()\n    ts.fit(train_logits, train_labels, val_logits, val_labels)\n    ts_probs = ts.calibrate(test_logits)\n    dataset_results['temperature_scaling'] = compute_metrics(ts_probs, test_labels)\n    \n    # Method 3: TEC\n    tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\n    tec.fit(train_logits, train_labels, val_logits, val_labels)\n    tec_probs = tec.calibrate(test_logits)\n    dataset_results['thermodynamic_entropy'] = compute_metrics(tec_probs, test_labels)\n    \n    # Method 4: Annealing + Softmax (with best params from validation)\n    best_params = tune_annealing_params(val_logits, val_labels)  # From Phase 2\n    annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(**best_params)\n    ann_probs = annealing.calibrate(test_logits)\n    dataset_results['annealing_softmax'] = compute_metrics(ann_probs, test_labels)\n    \n    # Method 5: Annealing + TEC\n    ann_tec = AnnealingPlusTEC(**best_params)\n    ann_tec.fit(train_logits, train_labels, val_logits, val_labels)\n    ann_tec_probs = ann_tec.calibrate(test_logits)\n    dataset_results['annealing_plus_tec'] = compute_metrics(ann_tec_probs, test_labels)\n    \n    results[dataset_name] = dataset_results\n    \n    # Print results\n    print(f\"\\nResults for {dataset_name}:\")\n    for method, metrics in dataset_results.items():\n        print(f\"  {method}:\")\n        print(f\"    Accuracy: {metrics['accuracy']:.4f}\")\n        print(f\"    ECE: {metrics['ece']:.4f}\")\n        print(f\"    Brier Score: {metrics['brier_score']:.4f}\")\n\n# Save results\nwith open('method_out.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(results, f, indent=2)\n\nprint(\"\\n\u2713 Experiment complete. Results saved to method_out.json\")\n```\n\n**Helper function to compute all metrics**:\n```python\ndef compute_metrics(probs, labels):\n    \"\"\"Compute all evaluation metrics for given probabilities and labels.\"\"\"\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\n    \n    accuracy = (preds == labels).float().mean().item()\n    ece = compute_ece(confs, preds, labels)\n    brier = compute_brier_score(probs, labels)\n    nll = compute_nll(probs, labels)\n    \n    return {\n        'accuracy': accuracy,\n        'ece': ece,\n        'brier_score': brier,\n        'nll': nll\n    }\n```\n\n### Phase 5: Statistical Significance (30 minutes)\n\n**Bootstrap confidence intervals**:\n```python\ndef bootstrap_ci(metric_fn, probs, labels, n_bootstrap=1000):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute 95% confidence interval using bootstrap resampling.\n    \n    Args:\n        metric_fn: Function that computes metric from probs and labels\n        probs: Probability predictions\n        labels: True labels\n        n_bootstrap: Number of bootstrap samples\n    \n    Returns:\n        (lower, upper): 95% confidence interval\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = len(labels)\n    scores = []\n    \n    for _ in range(n_bootstrap):\n        # Bootstrap sample (with replacement)\n        idx = torch.randint(0, n_samples, (n_samples,))\n        boot_probs = probs[idx]\n        boot_labels = labels[idx]\n        \n        # Compute metric\n        score = metric_fn(boot_probs, boot_labels)\n        scores.append(score)\n    \n    # Compute 2.5th and 97.5th percentiles\n    scores = sorted(scores)\n    lower = scores[int(0.025 * n_bootstrap)]\n    upper = scores[int(0.975 * n_bootstrap)]\n    \n    return (lower, upper)\n\n# Example usage\nprint(\"\\nComputing bootstrap CIs for ECE...\")\nfor method_name, method_probs in zip(['uncalibrated', 'ts', 'annealing'], [uncal_probs, ts_probs, ann_probs]):\n    ci_lower, ci_upper = bootstrap_ci(compute_ece, method_probs, test_labels)\n    print(f\"  {method_name}: ECE CI = [{ci_lower:.4f}, {ci_upper:.4f}]\")\n```\n\n**Paired t-test for method comparison**:\n```python\nfrom scipy import stats\n\ndef paired_ttest(method1_probs, method2_probs, labels):\n    \"\"\"\n    Paired t-test comparing two methods.\n    Null hypothesis: Methods have equal ECE.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Compute per-sample ECE contribution (using 10 bins)\n    n_samples = len(labels)\n    method1_ece_per_sample = compute_per_sample_ece(method1_probs, labels)\n    method2_ece_per_sample = compute_per_sample_ece(method2_probs, labels)\n    \n    # Paired t-test\n    t_stat, p_value = stats.ttest_rel(method1_ece_per_sample, method2_ece_per_sample)\n    \n    return t_stat, p_value\n\n# Example: Compare annealing vs temperature scaling\nt_stat, p_value = paired_ttest(ann_probs, ts_probs, test_labels)\nprint(f\"\\nPaired t-test (Annealing vs TS): t={t_stat:.3f}, p={p_value:.4f}\")\nif p_value < 0.05:\n    print(\"  Result: Statistically significant difference (p < 0.05)\")\nelse:\n    print(\"  Result: No statistically significant difference\")\n```\n\n### Phase 6: Visualization (30 minutes)\n\n**Reliability diagrams**:\n```python\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport seaborn as sns\n\ndef plot_reliability_diagram(confidences, predictions, labels, method_name, dataset_name):\n    \"\"\"Plot reliability diagram (accuracy vs confidence).\"\"\"\n    num_bins = 10\n    bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\n    \n    accuracies = []\n    confidences_bin = []\n    \n    for i in range(num_bins):\n        mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\n        if mask.sum() > 0:\n            acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\n            conf = confidences[mask].mean()\n            accuracies.append(acc.item())\n            confidences_bin.append(conf.item())\n        else:\n            accuracies.append(np.nan)\n            confidences_bin.append(np.nan)\n    \n    # Plot\n    plt.figure(figsize=(8, 6))\n    plt.plot([0, 1], [0, 1], 'k--', label='Perfect calibration')\n    plt.plot(confidences_bin, accuracies, 'o-', label=method_name)\n    plt.xlabel('Confidence')\n    plt.ylabel('Accuracy')\n    plt.title(f'Reliability Diagram: {method_name} on {dataset_name}')\n    plt.legend()\n    plt.grid(True)\n    plt.savefig(f'reliability_{method_name}_{dataset_name}.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n\n# Plot for each method\nfor method_name in ['uncalibrated', 'temperature_scaling', 'annealing_softmax']:\n    probs = all_probs[method_name]  # Load from results\n    preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\n    confs = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\n    plot_reliability_diagram(confs, preds, test_labels, method_name, dataset_name)\n```\n\n**Bar plot comparing ECE across methods**:\n```python\ndef plot_ece_comparison(results, dataset_name):\n    \"\"\"Bar plot of ECE for all methods.\"\"\"\n    methods = list(results[dataset_name].keys())\n    eces = [results[dataset_name][m]['ece'] for m in methods]\n    \n    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))\n    bars = plt.bar(methods, eces, color=['blue', 'green', 'orange', 'red', 'purple'])\n    plt.xlabel('Method')\n    plt.ylabel('Expected Calibration Error (ECE)')\n    plt.title(f'ECE Comparison on {dataset_name}')\n    plt.xticks(rotation=45, ha='right')\n    \n    # Add value labels on bars\n    for bar, ece in zip(bars, eces):\n        plt.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2, bar.get_height() + 0.001, \n                f'{ece:.4f}', ha='center', va='bottom')\n    \n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(f'ece_comparison_{dataset_name}.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n\nplot_ece_comparison(results, 'sst-2')\n```\n\n### Output Format\n\n**Save results to `method_out.json`**:\n```json\n{\n  \"experiment_name\": \"temperature_scaling\": {\"accuracy\": 0.852, \"ece\": 0.042, \"brier_score\": 0.231, \"nll\": 0.421},\n      \"annealing_softmax\": {\"accuracy\": 0.847, \"ece\": 0.058, \"brier_score\": 0.239, \"nll\": 0.438},\n      ...\n    },\n    \"ag_news\": {...},\n    \"dbpedia\": {...}\n  },\n  \"best_params\": {\n    \"annealing_softmax\": {\"T_start\": 2.0, \"T_end\": 1.0, \"schedule\": \"annealing_vs_uncalibrated_pvalue\": 0.008,\n    ...\n  },\n  \"visualizations\": [\n    \"reliability_uncalibrated_sst-2.png\",\n    \"ece_comparison_sst-2.png\",\n    ...\n  ],\n  \"execution_time\": {\n    \"total_seconds\": 12345,\n    \"per_dataset\": {...}\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Time Budget Allocation\n\n| Phase | Time | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| Phase 0: Setup | 30 min | Install deps, load data, load models |\n| Phase 1: Implementation | 1.5 hrs | Implement 5 calibration methods |\n| Phase 2: Hyperparameter search | 1.5 hrs | Tune annealing parameters on validation |\n| Phase 3: Evaluation | 45 min | Compute metrics on test set |\n| Phase 4: Statistical tests | 30 min | Bootstrap CIs, paired t-tests |\n| Phase 5: Visualization | 30 min | Reliability diagrams, bar plots |\n| Phase 6: Saving results | 15 min | Save to JSON, document findings |\n| **Buffer** | **1 hr** | **Contingency time** |\n| **Total** | **6 hrs** | **Within budget** |\n\n### Critical Implementation Details\n\n1. **Logit Access**: Use `model(**inputs).logits` with HuggingFace models. Ensure `return_dict=True` (default).\n\n2. **Numerical Stability**: Add small epsilon (`1e-10`) when computing log probabilities to avoid NaN.\n\n3. **Batch Processing**: Process data in batches (32-64) to avoid OOM. Forward pass, apply softmax to logits\n       probs = F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\n       preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\n       confidences = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\n       return preds, confidences, probs\n   ```\n\n2. **Temperature Scaling (TS)** - post-hoc:\n   ```python\n   class TemperatureScaling:\n       def __init__(self):\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\n       \n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n           # Optimize temperature on validation set using NLL loss\n           optimizer = torch.optim.LBFGS([self.temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\n           for _ in range(100):\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\n               scaled_logits = logits / self.temperature\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(scaled_logits, labels)\n               loss.backward()\n               optimizer.step(lambda: F.cross_entropy(logits / self.temperature, labels))\n           return self.temperature.item()\n       \n       def calibrate(self, logits):\n           return F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\n   ```\n\n3. **Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)** - post-hoc:\n   ```python\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\n       def __init__(self):\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\n       \n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\n           # Shannon entropy: H = -sum(p * log(p))\n           entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\n           return entropy\n       \n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n           # Optimize temperature and entropy_weight on validation set\n           # TEC formula: calibrated_probs = softmax(logits / T) * entropy_adjustment\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\n           for epoch in range(100):\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\n               scaled_logits = logits / self.temperature\n               probs = F.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\n               # Adjust probabilities based on entropy\n               adjusted_probs = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\n               adjusted_probs = adjusted_probs / adjusted_probs.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted_probs + 1e-10), labels)\n               loss.backward()\n               optimizer.step()\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\n   ```\n\n### Phase 2: Inference-Time Temperature Annealing (Core Novelty)\n\n1. **Implement temperature annealing during forward pass**:\n   ```python\n   def anneal_temperature(class_idx, num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\n       \"\"\"\n       Compute annealed temperature for each class.\n       T(c) = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule(c / C)\n       where c indexes classes [0, C)\n       \"\"\"\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\n       x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\n       \n       if schedule_type == 'linear':\n           # schedule(x) = 1 - x\n           schedule = 1.0 - x\n       elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\n           # schedule(x) = exp(-x)\n           schedule = torch.exp(-x)\n       elif schedule_type == 'physics':\n           # schedule(x) = 1 / log(1 + x * (e - 1))\n           schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\n       else:\n           raise ValueError(f\"Unknown schedule: {schedule_type}\")\n       \n       T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\n       return T_c  # Shape: (num_classes,)\n   ```\n\n2. **Annealing + Softmax (Method 3)**:\n   ```python\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\n           self.T_start = T_start\n           self.T_end = T_end\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\n       \n       def calibrate(self, logits):\n           \"\"\"\n           Apply temperature annealing during inference.\n           For each sample, compute per-class temperatures and scale logits.\n           \"\"\"\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(\n               class_idx=None,  # Apply to all classes\n               num_classes=num_classes,\n               T_start=self.T_start,\n               T_end=self.T_end,\n               schedule_type=self.schedule_type\n           )  # Shape: (num_classes,)\n           \n           # Expand to batch size\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)  # (batch, classes)\n           \n           # Scale logits by per-class temperature\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\n           \n           # Apply softmax\n           probs = F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\n           return probs\n   ```\n\n3. **Annealing + Post-hoc TEC (Method 4)**:\n   ```python\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\n       \n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\n           # First apply annealing\n           annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\n           val_annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\n           \n           # Then fit TEC on annealed probabilities (convert back to logits)\n           annealed_logits = torch.log(annealed_probs + 1e-10)\n           val_annealed_logits = torch.log(val_annealed_probs + 1e-10)\n           \n           T_opt, w_opt = self.tec.fit(annealed_logits, labels, val_annealed_logits, val_labels)\n           return T_opt, w_opt\n       \n       def calibrate(self, logits):\n           annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\n           # Forward pass, apply softmax to logits\\n       probs = F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\\n       preds = torch.argmax(probs, dim=-1)\\n       confidences = torch.max(probs, dim=-1).values\\n       return preds, confidences, probs\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Temperature Scaling (TS)** - post-hoc:\\n   ```python\\n   class TemperatureScaling:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n       \\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           # Optimize temperature on validation set using NLL loss\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.LBFGS([self.temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n           for _ in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               scaled_logits = logits / self.temperature\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(scaled_logits, labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step(lambda: F.cross_entropy(logits / self.temperature, labels))\\n           return self.temperature.item()\\n       \\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           return F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC)** - post-hoc:\\n   ```python\\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\\n       \\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           # Shannon entropy: H = -sum(p * log(p))\\n           entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n           return entropy\\n       \\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           # Optimize temperature and entropy_weight on validation set\\n           # TEC formula: calibrated_probs = softmax(logits / T) * entropy_adjustment\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\\n           for epoch in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               scaled_logits = logits / self.temperature\\n               probs = F.softmax(scaled_logits, dim=-1)\\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\\n               # Adjust probabilities based on entropy\\n               adjusted_probs = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n               adjusted_probs = adjusted_probs / adjusted_probs.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted_probs + 1e-10), labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step()\\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\\n   ```\\n\\n### Phase 2: Inference-Time Temperature Annealing (Core Novelty)\\n\\n1. **Implement temperature annealing during forward pass**:\\n   ```python\\n   def anneal_temperature(class_idx, num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\\n       \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n       Compute annealed temperature for each class.\\n       T(c) = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule(c / C)\\n       where c indexes classes [0, C)\\n       \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\\n       x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\\n       \\n       if schedule_type == 'linear':\\n           # schedule(x) = 1 - x\\n           schedule = 1.0 - x\\n       elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\\n           # schedule(x) = exp(-x)\\n           schedule = torch.exp(-x)\\n       elif schedule_type == 'physics':\\n           # schedule(x) = 1 / log(1 + x * (e - 1))\\n           schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\\n       else:\\n           raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown schedule: {schedule_type}\\\")\\n       \\n       T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\\n       return T_c  # Shape: (num_classes,)\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Annealing + Softmax (Method 3)**:\\n   ```python\\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.T_start = T_start\\n           self.T_end = T_end\\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\\n       \\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n           Apply temperature annealing during inference.\\n           For each sample, compute per-class temperatures and scale logits.\\n           \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(\\n               class_idx=None,  # Apply to all classes\\n               num_classes=num_classes,\\n               T_start=self.T_start,\\n               T_end=self.T_end,\\n               schedule_type=self.schedule_type\\n           )  # Shape: (num_classes,)\\n           \\n           # Expand to batch size\\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)  # (batch, classes)\\n           \\n           # Scale logits by per-class temperature\\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\\n           \\n           # Apply softmax\\n           probs = F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\\n           return probs\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Annealing + Post-hoc TEC (Method 4)**:\\n   ```python\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\n       \\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           # First apply annealing\\n           annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           val_annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\n           \\n           # Then fit TEC on annealed probabilities (convert back to logits)\\n           annealed_logits = torch.log(annealed_probs + 1e-10)\\n           val_annealed_logits = torch.log(val_annealed_probs + 1e-10)\\n           \\n           T_opt, w_opt = self.tec.fit(annealed_logits, labels, val_annealed_logits, val_labels)\\n           return T_opt, w_opt\\n       \\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           annealed_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           # Apply TEC adjustment\\n           entropy = self.tec.compute_entropy(annealed_probs)\\n           adjusted = annealed_probs * (1 + self.tec.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n       <response clipped><NOTE>Due to the max output limit, only part of this file has been shown to you. METHOD 4 - ANNEALING + SOFTMAX (CORE NOVELTY):\\\\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\\\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\\\n           self.T_start = T_start\\\\n           self.T_end = T_end\\\\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\\\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\\\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\\\\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes, self.T_start, self.T_end, self.schedule_type)\\\\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)\\\\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\\\\n           return F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\\\\n\\\\n6. METHOD 5 - ANNEALING + TEC:\\\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\\\n           ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\\\n           val_ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\\\n           ann_logits = torch.log(ann_probs + 1e-10)\\\\n           val_ann_logits = torch.log(val_ann_probs + 1e-10)\\\\n           return self.tec.fit(ann_logits, labels, val_ann_logits, val_labels)\\\\n\\\\nPHASE 2: HYPERPARAMETER SEARCH (1.5 hrs)\\\\n====================================\\\\nGrid search over:\\\\n  T_start in {1.0, 2.0, 5.0}\\\\n  T_end in {0.5, 1.0}\\\\n  schedule_type in {linear, exponential, physics}\\\\n\\\\nUse VALIDATION set for tuning (NOT test set).\\\\nSelect params with lowest ECE on val set.\\\\n\\\\nPHASE 3: EVALUATION METRICS (45 min)\\\\n=================================\\\\n\\\\n1. ECE (Expected Calibration Error):\\\\n   def compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\\\\n       bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\\\\n       ece = 0.0\\\\n       for i in range(num_bins):\\\\n           mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\\\\n           if mask.sum() > 0:\\\\n               bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\\\\n               bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\\\\n               ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\\\\n       return ece.item()\\\\n\\\\n2. Brier Score:\\\\n   def compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\\\\n       one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=probs.shape[-1]).float()\\\\n       return torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2).item()\\\\n\\\\n3. NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood):\\\\n   def compute_nll(probs, labels):\\\\n       return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\\\\n\\\\nPHASE 4: RUN EXPERIMENTS (1.5 hrs)\\\\n=============================\\\\nFor each dataset (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\\\\n  1. METHOD 3 - Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC):\\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           return -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\\n           for epoch in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               probs = F.softmax(val_logits / self.temperature, dim=-1)\\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\\n               adjusted = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n               adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted + 1e-10), val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step()\\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\\n\\n5. METHOD 4 - Annealing + Softmax (CORE NOVELTY):\\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.T_start = T_start\\n           self.T_end = T_end\\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes, self.T_start, self.T_end, self.schedule_type)\\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)\\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\\n           return F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\\n\\n6. METHOD 5 - Annealing + TEC:\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           val_ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\n           ann_logits = torch.log(ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           val_ann_logits = torch.log(val_ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           return self.tec.fit(ann_logits, labels, val_ann_logits, val_labels)\\n\\nPHASE 2: HYPERPARAMETER SEARCH (1.5 hours)\\n============================================\\nGrid search over annealing parameters:\\n  T_start in {1.0, 2.0, 5.0}\\n  T_end in {0.5, 1.0}\\n  schedule_type in {linear, exponential, physics}\\n\\nUse VALIDATION set for tuning (NOT test set).\\nSelect params with lowest ECE on validation set.\\n\\nPHASE 3: EVALUATION METRICS (45 minutes)\\n=======================================\\n\\n1. ECE (Expected Calibration Error):\\n   def compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\\n       bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\\n       ece = 0.0\\n       for i in range(num_bins):\\n           mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\\n           if mask.sum() > 0:\\n               bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\\n               bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\\n               ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\\n       return ece.item()\\n\\n2. Brier Score:\\n   def compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\\n       one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=probs.shape[-1]).float()\\n       return torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2).item()\\n\\n3. NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood):\\n   def compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n       return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\\n\\nPHASE 4: RUN EXPERIMENTS (1.5 hours)\\n====================================\\nFor each dataset (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\\n  1. Load data and pretrained model\\n  2. Get logits for train/val/test sets\\n  3. Fit each method on train set, tune on val set\\n  4. Evaluate all methods on test set\\n  5. Record metrics: accuracy, ECE, Brier score, NLL\\n\\nOutput format (save to method_out.json):\\n{\\n  \\\"experiment_name\\\": \\\"inference_time_temperature_annealing\\\",\\n  \\\"datasets\\\": [\\\"sst-2\\\", \\\"ag_news\\\", \\\"dbpedia\\\"],\\n  \\\"methods\\\": [\\\"uncalibrated\\\", \\\"temperature_scaling\\\", \\\"thermodynamic_entropy\\\", \\\"annealing_softmax\\\", \\\"annealing_plus_tec\\\"],\\n  \\\"results\\\": {\\n    \\\"sst-2\\\": {\\n      \\\"uncalibrated\\\": {\\\"accuracy\\\": 0.85, \\\"ece\\\": 0.12, \\\"brier_score\\\": 0.25, \\\"nll\\\": 0.45},\\n      \\\"temperature_scaling\\\": {...},\\n      ...\\n    },\\n    ...\\n  },\\n  \\\"best_params\\\": {...},\\n  \\\"statistical_tests\\\": {...},\\n  \\\"visualizations\\\": [...]\\n}\\n\\nPHASE 5: STATISTICAL SIGNIFICANCE (30 minutes)\\n============================================\\n1. Reliability diagrams (accuracy vs confidence plots)\\n2. CORE FUNCTION - Temperature Annealing:\\n   def anneal_temperature(num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\\n       x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\\n       if schedule_type == 'linear':\\n           schedule = 1.0 - x\\n       elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\\n           schedule = torch.exp(-x)\\n       elif schedule_type == 'physics':\\n           schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\\n       T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\\n       return T_c  # Shape: (num_classes,)\\n\\n2. METHOD 3 - Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC):\\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           return -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\\n           for epoch in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               probs = F.softmax(val_logits / self.temperature, dim=-1)\\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\\n               adjusted = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n               adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted + 1e-10), val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step()\\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\\n\\n5. METHOD 5 - Annealing + TEC:\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           val_ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\n           ann_logits = torch.log(ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           val_ann_logits = torch.log(val_ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           return self.tec.fit(ann_logits, labels, val_ann_logits, val_labels)\\n\\nPHASE 2: HYPERPARAMETER SEARCH (1.5 hours)\\n============================================\\nGrid search over annealing parameters:\\n  T_start in {1.0, 2.0, 5.0}\\n  T_end in {0.5, 1.0}\\n  schedule_type in {linear, exponential, physics}\\n\\nUse VALIDATION set for tuning (NOT test set).\\nSelect params with lowest ECE on validation set.\\n\\nPHASE 3: EVALUATION METRICS (45 minutes)\\n=======================================\\n\\n1. ECE (Expected Calibration Error):\\n   def compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\\n       bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\\n       ece = 0.0\\n       for i in range(num_bins):\\n           mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\\n           if mask.sum() > 0:\\n               bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\\n               bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\\n               ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\\n       return ece.item()\\n\\n2. Brier Score:\\n   def compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\\n       one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=probs.shape[-1]).float()\\n       return torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2).item()\\n\\n3. NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood):\\n   def compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n       return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\\n\\nPHASE 4: RUN EXPERIMENTS (1.5 hours)\\n====================================\\nFor each dataset (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\\n  1. Uncalibrated baseline: Standard softmax on logits\\n  2. Temperature Scaling (TS): Post-hoc calibration with single temperature\\n  3. Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC): Post-hoc using entropy adjustments\\n  4. Annealing + Softmax: Inference-time per-class temperature annealing (CORE NOVELTY)\\n  5. Annealing + TEC: Combine annealing with post-hoc TEC\\n\\nKEY TECHNICAL CHALLENGE: Need access to LOGITS (pre-softmax activations).\\n- OpenRouter APIs don't expose logits -> Use LOCAL HuggingFace models.\\n- Load models in evaluation mode, extract model(**inputs).logits\\n\\nPHASE 0: SETUP (30 minutes)\\n=============================\\n1. CORE FUNCTION - Temperature Annealing:\\n   def anneal_temperature(num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\\n       x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\\n       if schedule_type == 'linear':\\n           schedule = 1.0 - x\\n       elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\\n           schedule = torch.exp(-x)\\n       elif schedule_type == 'physics':\\n           schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\\n       T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\\n       return T_c  # Shape: (num_classes,)\\n\\n2. METHOD 1 - Uncalibrated Baseline:\\n   def uncalibrated_predict(logits):\\n       return F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\\n\\n3. METHOD 2 - Temperature Scaling (TS):\\n   class TemperatureScaling:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.LBFGS([self.temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n           for _ in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(val_logits / self.temperature, val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step(lambda: F.cross_entropy(val_logits / self.temperature, val_labels))\\n           return self.temperature.item()\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           return F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\\n\\n4. METHOD 3 - Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC):\\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           return -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\\n           for epoch in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               probs = F.softmax(val_logits / self.temperature, dim=-1)\\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\\n               adjusted = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n               adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted + 1e-10), val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step()\\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\\n\\n5. METHOD 4 - Annealing + Softmax (CORE NOVELTY):\\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.T_start = T_start\\n           self.T_end = T_end\\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes, self.T_start, self.T_end, self.schedule_type)\\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)\\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\\n           return F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\\n\\n6. METHOD 5 - Annealing + TEC:\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           val_ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\n           ann_logits = torch.log(ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           val_ann_logits = torch.log(val_ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           return self.tec.fit(ann_logits, labels, val_ann_logits, val_labels)\\n\\nPHASE 2: HYPERPARAMETER SEARCH (1.5 hours)\\n============================================\\nGrid search over annealing parameters:\\n  T_start in {1.0, 2.0, 5.0}\\n  T_end in {0.5, 1.0}\\n  schedule_type in {linear, exponential, physics}\\n\\nUse VALIDATION set for tuning (NOT test set).\\nSelect params with lowest ECE on validation set.\\n\\nPHASE 3: EVALUATION METRICS (45 minutes)\\n=======================================\\n\\n1. ECE (Expected Calibration Error):\\n   def compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\\n       bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\\n       ece = 0.0\\n       for i in range(num_bins):\\n           mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\\n           if mask.sum() > 0:\\n               bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\\n               bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\\n               ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\\n       return ece.item()\\n\\n2. Brier Score:\\n   def compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\\n       one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=probs.shape[-1]).float()\\n       return torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2).item()\\n\\n3. NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood):\\n   def compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n       return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\\n\\nPHASE 4: RUN EXPERIMENTS (1.5 hours)\\n====================================\\nFor each dataset (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\\n  1. \\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           # Shannon entropy: H = -sum(p * log(p))\\n           entropy = -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n           return T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule(c / C)\\n       where c indexes classes [0, C)\\n       \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\\n       x = c / num_classes  #   "file_text": "{\n  \"title\": \"Test temperature annealing for LLM calibration\",\n  \"summary\": \"Implement and evaluate inference-time temperature annealing during LLM classification, comparing against standard temperature scaling and thermodynamic entropy calibration methods on SST-2, AG News, and DBpedia datasets.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"gpu\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"EXPERIMENT PLAN: Temperature Annealing for LLM Calibration\\n\\nOVERVIEW\\n=========\\nEvaluate inference-time temperature annealing (core novelty from hypothesis) vs post-hoc calibration methods.\\n\\nDATASETS: SST-2 (2 classes), AG News (4 classes), DBpedia (14 classes)\\nMETHODS TO COMPARE:\\n  1. Uncalibrated baseline: Standard softmax on logits\\n  2. Temperature Scaling (TS): Post-hoc calibration with single temperature\\n  3. Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC): Post-hoc using entropy adjustments\\n  4. Annealing + Softmax: Inference-time per-class temperature annealing (CORE NOVELTY)\\n  5. Annealing + TEC: Combine annealing with post-hoc TEC\\n\\nKEY TECHNICAL CHALLENGE: Need access to LOGITS (pre-softmax activations).\\n- OpenRouter APIs don't expose logits -> Use LOCAL HuggingFace models.\\n- Load models in evaluation mode, extract model(**inputs).logits\\n\\nPHASE 0: SETUP (30 minutes)\\n=============================\\n1. Install dependencies:\\n   pip install torch transformers datasets numpy pandas scikit-learn matplotlib seaborn tqdm\\n\\n2. Load datasets from dependency artifact:\\n   Path: /ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_3fUR0i5e8NC7/3_invention_loop/iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json\\n   Use 3 datasets: SST-2, AG News, DBpedia\\n   Create train/val/test splits: 70%/15%/15% with STRATIFIED sampling\\n\\n3. Load pretrained models (local, for logit access):\\n   - SST-2: textattack/bert-base-uncased-SST-2\\n   - AG News: textattack/roberta-base-ag-news\\n   - DBpedia: Train simple classifier on sentence embeddings (see fallback plan)\\n\\nPHASE 1: IMPLEMENT CALIBRATION METHODS (1.5 hours)\\n====================================================\\n\\n1. CORE FUNCTION - Temperature Annealing:\\n   def anneal_temperature(num_classes, T_start, T_end, schedule_type):\\n       c = torch.arange(num_classes, dtype=torch.float32)\\n       x = c / num_classes  # Normalized class index in [0, 1]\\n       if schedule_type == 'linear':\\n           schedule = 1.0 - x\\n       elif schedule_type == 'exponential':\\n           schedule = torch.exp(-x)\\n       elif schedule_type == 'physics':\\n           schedule = 1.0 / torch.log(1 + x * (torch.e - 1))\\n       T_c = T_end + (T_start - T_end) * schedule\\n       return T_c  # Shape: (num_classes,)\\n\\n2. METHOD 1 - Uncalibrated Baseline:\\n   def uncalibrated_predict(logits):\\n       return F.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\\n\\n3. METHOD 2 - Temperature Scaling (TS):\\n   class TemperatureScaling:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.LBFGS([self.temperature], lr=0.01, max_iter=50)\\n           for _ in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(val_logits / self.temperature, val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step(lambda: F.cross_entropy(val_logits / self.temperature, val_labels))\\n           return self.temperature.item()\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           return F.softmax(logits / self.temperature.item(), dim=-1)\\n\\n4. METHOD 3 - Thermodynamic Entropy Calibration (TEC):\\n   class ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration:\\n       def __init__(self):\\n           self.temperature = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * 1.0)\\n           self.entropy_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1))\\n       def compute_entropy(self, probs):\\n           return -torch.sum(probs * torch.log(probs + 1e-10), dim=-1)\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           optimizer = torch.optim.Adam([self.temperature, self.entropy_weight], lr=0.01)\\n           for epoch in range(100):\\n               optimizer.zero_grad()\\n               probs = F.softmax(val_logits / self.temperature, dim=-1)\\n               entropy = self.compute_entropy(probs)\\n               adjusted = probs * (1 + self.entropy_weight * entropy.unsqueeze(-1))\\n               adjusted = adjusted / adjusted.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\\n               loss = F.cross_entropy(torch.log(adjusted + 1e-10), val_labels)\\n               loss.backward()\\n               optimizer.step()\\n           return self.temperature.item(), self.entropy_weight.item()\\n\\n5. METHOD 4 - Annealing + Softmax (CORE NOVELTY):\\n   class AnnealingSoftmax:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.T_start = T_start\\n           self.T_end = T_end\\n           self.schedule_type = schedule_type\\n       def calibrate(self, logits):\\n           num_classes = logits.shape[-1]\\n           T_c = anneal_temperature(num_classes, self.T_start, self.T_end, self.schedule_type)\\n           T_c_batch = T_c.unsqueeze(0).expand(logits.shape[0], -1)\\n           annealed_logits = logits / T_c_batch\\n           return F.softmax(annealed_logits, dim=-1)\\n\\n6. METHOD 5 - Annealing + TEC:\\n   class AnnealingPlusTEC:\\n       def __init__(self, T_start=2.0, T_end=1.0, schedule_type='linear'):\\n           self.annealing = AnnealingSoftmax(T_start, T_end, schedule_type)\\n           self.tec = ThermodynamicEntropyCalibration()\\n       def fit(self, logits, labels, val_logits, val_labels):\\n           ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(logits)\\n           val_ann_probs = self.annealing.calibrate(val_logits)\\n           ann_logits = torch.log(ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           val_ann_logits = torch.log(val_ann_probs + 1e-10)\\n           return self.tec.fit(ann_logits, labels, val_ann_logits, val_labels)\\n\\nPHASE 2: HYPERPARAMETER SEARCH (1.5 hours)\\n============================================\\nGrid search over annealing parameters:\\n  T_start in {1.0, 2.0, 5.0}\\n  T_end in {0.5, 1.0}\\n  schedule_type in {linear, exponential, physics}\\n\\nUse VALIDATION set for tuning (NOT test set).\\nSelect params with lowest ECE on validation set.\\n\\nPHASE 3: EVALUATION METRICS (45 minutes)\\n=======================================\\n\\n1. ECE (Expected Calibration Error):\\n   def compute_ece(confidences, predictions, labels, num_bins=10):\\n       bins = torch.linspace(0, 1, num_bins + 1)\\n       ece = 0.0\\n       for i in range(num_bins):\\n           mask = (confidences >= bins[i]) & (confidences < bins[i+1])\\n           if mask.sum() > 0:\\n               bin_conf = confidences[mask].mean()\\n               bin_acc = (predictions[mask] == labels[mask]).float().mean()\\n               ece += (mask.sum().float() / len(confidences)) * torch.abs(bin_acc - bin_conf)\\n       return ece.item()\\n\\n2. Brier Score:\\n   def compute_brier_score(probs, labels):\\n       one_hot = F.one_hot(labels, num_classes=probs.shape[-1]).float()\\n       return torch.mean((probs - one_hot) ** 2).item()\\n\\n3. NLL (Negative Log-Likelihood):\\n   def compute_nll(probs, labels):\\n       return F.nll_loss(torch.log(probs + 1e-10), labels).item()\\n\\nPHASE 4: RUN EXPERIMENTS (1.5 hours)\\n====================================\\nFor each dataset (SST-2, AG News, DBpedia):\\n  1. Load data and pretrained model\\n  2. Get logits for train/val/test sets\\n  3. Fit each method on train set, tune on val set\\n  4. Evaluate all methods on test set\\n  5. Record metrics: accuracy, ECE, Brier score, NLL\\n\\nOutput format (save to method_out.json):\\n{\\n  \\\"experiment_name\\\": \\\"inference_time_temperature_annealing\\\",\\n  \\\"datasets\\\": [\\\"sst-2\\\", \\\"ag_news\\\", \\\"dbpedia\\\"],\\n  \\\"methods\\\": [\\\"uncalibrated\\\", \\\"temperature_scaling\\\", \\\"thermodynamic_entropy\\\", \\\"annealing_softmax\\\", \\\"annealing_plus_tec\\\"],\\n  \\\"results\\\": {\\n    \\\"sst-2\\\": {\\n      \\\"uncalibrated\\\": {\\\"accuracy\\\": 0.85, \\\"ece\\\": 0.12, \\\"brier_score\\\": 0.25, \\\"nll\\\": 0.45},\\n      \\\"temperature_scaling\\\": {...},\\n      ...\\n    },\\n    ...\\n  },\\n  \\\"best_params\\\": {...},\\n  \\\"statistical_tests\\\": {...},\\n  \\\"visualizations\\\": [...]\\n}\\n\\nPHASE 5: STATISTICAL SIGNIFICANCE (30 minutes)\\n============================================\\n1.
